i want to share with you some ideas about the secret power of time , in a very short time .	我想和大家分享一些關於時間的秘密力量的想法 , 在很短的時間內 。
video: all right , start the clock please . 30 seconds studio .	影片:好的 , 開始時鐘 。 三十秒的工作室 。
keep it quiet please . settle down .	讓它安靜下來 。 安頓下來 。
it's about time . end sequence . take one .	時間到了 , 終結序列 。 拿一個 。
10 , nine , eight , seven , six , five , four , three , two . . .	10、9、8、7、6、5、4、3、2......
philip zimbardo: let's tune into the conversation of the principals in adam's temptation .	菲利普•辛巴多:咱們來談談亞當的誘惑 。
" come on adam , don't be so wishywashy . take a bite . " " i did . "	「 拜託 , 不要太清醒了 。 拿一點點 。 」 我真的 。
" one bite , adam . don't abandon eve . "	「 一咬 , 亞當 , 別放棄eve 。 」
" i don't know , guys .	「 我不知道 , 各位 。
i don't want to get in trouble . "	我不想惹麻煩 。 」
" okay . one bite . what the hell ? "	「 好吧 , 來吧 。 來吧 。 來吧 ? 」
life is temptation . it's all about yielding , resisting , yes , no , now , later , impulsive , reflective , present focus and future focus .	生命是誘惑 。 一切都有關生育、抗拒 , 是的 , 不 , 之後 , 衝動、現在和未來的焦點 。
promised virtues fall prey to the passions of the moment .	承諾美德會陷入當下的熱情 。
of teenage girls who pledged sexual abstinence and virginity until marriage thank you george bush the majority , 60 percent , yielded to sexual temptations within one year .	在十幾歲的女孩中 , 她們的性缺陷和處女緊張 , 直到婚姻 , 感謝你喬治布希主要 , 百分之六十 , 一年內就被性誘惑 。
and most of them did so without using birth control .	大部份的確不用生育控制 。
so much for promises .	許多的承諾 。
now lets tempt fouryearolds , giving them a treat .	現在讓我們嘗試四歲的孩子 , 給他們一個治療 。
they can have one marshmallow now . but if they wait until the experimenter comes back , they can have two .	他們現在可以有一顆棉花糖 , 但如果他們等到實驗人員回來 , 他們就可以有兩顆 。
of course it pays , if you like marshmallows , to wait .	當然 , 要是你喜歡棉花糖 , 才能等待 。
what happens is twothirds of the kids give in to temptation .	接下來發生的是三分之二的孩子給予誘惑 。
they cannot wait . the others , of course , wait .	他們不能等 。 其他人 , 當然 , 等等 。
they resist the temptation . they delay the now for later .	他們抗拒誘惑 , 等一下會延遲 。
walter mischel , my colleague at stanford , went back 14 years later , to try to discover what was different about those kids .	我在史丹佛的同事華特.米歇爾 , 14年後回到過去 , 試著去了解那些孩子的不同之處 。
there were enormous differences between kids who resisted and kids who yielded , in many ways .	有很大的差別 , 那些抗拒和孩子的差別在很多方面都有 。
the kids who resisted scored 250 points higher on the sat .	那些抗拒評分的孩子在現場高達250分 。
that's enormous . that's like a whole set of different iq points .	這很巨大 。 這就像是一整組不同的智商點 。
they didn't get in as much trouble . they were better students .	他們沒有遇到太多麻煩 , 他們是更好的學生 。
they were selfconfident and determined . and the key for me today , the key for you , is , they were futurefocused rather than presentfocused .	他們是自信和決心 , 今天我要給你們的關鍵 , 是他們是未來的專注 , 而不是現在 。
so what is time perspective ? that's what i'm going to talk about today .	所以 , 時間的觀點是什麼 ? 這就是我今天要談的 。
time perspective is the study of how individuals , all of us , divide the flow of your human experience into time zones or time categories .	時間的觀點是研究個人、我們所有人 , 將你人類的經驗分割成時間區或時間分類 。
and you do it automatically and nonconsciously .	而你會自動且無意識地做它 。
they vary between cultures , between nations , between individuals , between social classes , between education levels .	他們在文化、國家之間、個人、社會階級、教育層面之間的差異 。
and the problem is that they can become biased , because you learn to overuse some of them and underuse the others .	問題是 , 它們可以變得偏見 , 因為你學會過度使用它們 , 用其他的 。
what determines any decision you make ?	你做了什麼決定 ?
you make a decision on which you're going to base an action .	你做了一個決定 , 決定你要採取行動 。
for some people it's only about what is in the immediate situation , what other people are doing and what you're feeling .	對某些人來說 , 只有在當下的情況下 , 其他人在做什麼 , 及你感受到什麼 。
and those people , when they make their decisions in that format we're going to call them " presentoriented , " because their focus is what is now .	那些人 , 當他們在那樣的形式下做出決定時 , 我們會稱他們為 「 現狀 」 , 因為他們的焦點是現在的 。
for others , the present is irrelevant .	對其他人來說 , 現在是不相關的 。
it's always about " what is this situation like that i've experienced in the past ? "	總是在說 「 我過去經歷過的情況是什麼 ? 」
so that their decisions are based on past memories .	所以 , 他們的決定是基於過去的記憶 。
and we're going to call those people " pastoriented , " because they focus on what was .	我們將稱這些人為 「 放牧 」 , 因為他們專注於什麼 。
for others it's not the past , it's not the present , it's only about the future .	對其他人來說 , 不是過去 , 不是現在 , 而是關於未來 。
their focus is always about anticipated consequences .	他們的焦點總是在預期後的結果 。
we're going to call them " futureoriented . " their focus is on what will be .	我們稱他們為 「 未來主義 」 , 他們的焦點在將來會是什麼 。
so , time paradox , i want to argue , the paradox of time perspective , is something that influences every decision you make , you're totally unaware of .	所以 , 時間悖論 , 我想主張 , 時間的觀點 , 是影響你做出的每一個決定 , 你完全不知道的 。
namely , the extent to which you have one of these biased time perspectives .	也就是說 , 你有這種偏見時間觀點的程度 。
well there is actually six of them . there are two ways to be presentoriented .	其實有六個 。 有兩種方式可以被呈現出來 。
there is two ways to be pastoriented , two ways to be future .	有兩種方式可以被放牧 , 有兩種方式可以成為未來 。
you can focus on pastpositive , or pastnegative .	你可以把焦點放在正面或負面的 。
you can be presenthedonistic , namely you focus on the joys of life , or presentfatalist it doesn't matter , your life is controlled .	你可以是現代主義者 , 即你把焦點放在人生的喜悅或現代主義者 , 這無所謂 , 你的人生被控制著 。
you can be futureoriented , setting goals .	你可以是未來的、設定的目標 。
or you can be transcendental future: namely , life begins after death .	或者 , 你可以是超自然的未來:生命始於死亡後 。
developing the mental flexibility to shift time perspectives fluidly depending on the demands of the situation , that's what you've got to learn to do .	開發靈活性 , 讓時間的觀點流暢地依據情況的需求 , 這就是你要學會做的事 。
so , very quickly , what is the optimal time profile ?	很快地 , 最佳時光檔案是什麼 ?
high on pastpositive . moderately high on future .	高度正面 。 未來的高度 。
and moderate on presenthedonism .	還有現代主義的現代主義 。
and always low on pastnegative and presentfatalism .	總是低於負面和現代主義 。
so the optimal temporal mix is what you get from the past pastpositive gives you roots . you connect your family , identity and your self .	所以 , 最佳的暫停混合是你從過去的假設給予你根 。 你將你的家人、身份和你的自我連結起來 。
what you get from the future is wings to soar to new destinations , new challenges .	你從未來得到的就是翅膀 , 到新的目的地 , 新的挑戰 。
what you get from the present hedonism is the energy , the energy to explore yourself , places , people , sensuality .	你從現在的衛生主義得到的就是能量 , 去探索自己、地點、人、感知能力 。
any time perspective in excess has more negatives than positives .	任何時間的觀點都比正面的負面值高 。
what do futures sacrifice for success ?	未來如何犧牲成功 ?
they sacrifice family time . they sacrifice friend time .	他們犧牲家人的時間 , 犧牲朋友的時間 。
they sacrifice fun time . they sacrifice personal indulgence .	它們犧牲了好玩的時間 , 它們犧牲了個人的成分 。
they sacrifice hobbies . and they sacrifice sleep . so it affects their health .	它們犧牲了嗜好 , 它們犧牲了睡眠 。 所以它會影響他們的健康 。
and they live for work , achievement and control .	他們活在工作上 , 成就和控制 。
i'm sure that resonates with some of the tedsters .	我確信和一些ted的演說會產生共鳴 。
and it resonated for me . i grew up as a poor kid in the south bronx ghetto , a sicilian family everyone lived in the past and present .	這對我產生共鳴 。 我在南布朗克斯•蓋茨托長大 , 一位西尼亞家庭 , 所有人都住在過去和現在 。
i'm here as a futureoriented person who went over the top , who did all these sacrifices because teachers intervened , and made me future oriented .	我來到這裡 , 身為一個有前途的人 , 走過頂部 , 做這些犧牲 , 是因為老師介入 , 讓我成為未來的方向 。
told me don't eat that marshmallow , because if you wait you're going to get two of them , until i learned to balance out .	告訴我不要吃棉花糖 , 因為如果你等你拿到兩顆 , 直到我學會了平衡 。
i've added presenthedonism , i've added a focus on the pastpositive , so , at 76 years old , i am more energetic than ever , more productive , and i'm happier than i have ever been .	我加入了簡報主義 , 我把焦點放在 「 偽證 」 上 , 在76歲時 , 我比以前更活躍 , 更有生產力 , 我比以前更快樂 。
i just want to say that we are applying this to many world problems: changing the dropout rates of school kids , combating addictions , enhancing teen health , curing vets' ptsd with time metaphors getting miracle cures promoting sustainability and conservation , reducing physical rehabilitation where there is a 50percent drop out rate , altering appeals to suicidal terrorists , and modifying family conflicts as timezone clashes .	我只想說 , 我們應用在許多世界問題上:改變學校的輟學率 , 加強青少年健康 , 策劃創投者得到奇蹟的比喻 , 促進了永續發展和保育 , 降低了實體復甦率 , 超過50% , 讓自殺的恐怖份子變得更恐怖主義 , 改變了家人的衝突 , 轉變為時代時代的衝突 。
so i want to end by saying: many of life's puzzles can be solved by understanding your time perspective and that of others .	最後我想說的是:許多生命的謎題可以透過了解你的時間觀和其他人的觀點來解決 。
and the idea is so simple , so obvious , but i think the consequences are really profound .	這個想法很簡單 , 很明顯 , 但我認為後果是很深刻的 。
how many of today's headlines will matter in 100 years ? 1000 ? kirk citron's " long news " project collects stories that not only matter today , but will resonate for decades even centuries to come . at ted2010 , he highlights recent headlines with the potential to shape our future .	一百年後 , 今天的頭條有多少 ? 一百元 ? 克爾克•克倫的《漫長新聞》計畫收集了現今重要的故事 , 數十年來 , 甚至在ted2010年 , 他針對我們未來的潛力標題 。
future , global issues , media , news , science	未來 , 全球議題、媒體、新聞、科學、科學、科學、科學等問題 。
kirk citron: and now , the real news	kirkcitron:現在 , 真正的消息是 , 真正的消息 。
we are drowning in news .	我們在新聞中淹沒了 。
reuters alone puts out three and a half million news stories a year .	光是路易斯 , 每年就有三百五十萬則新聞報導 。
that's just one source .	這只是其中一個來源 。
my question is: how many of those stories are actually going to matter in the long run ?	我的問題是:長期來說 , 當中有多少故事會發生在哪裡 ?
that's the idea behind the long news .	這就是長期新聞背後的想法 。
it's a project by the long now foundation , which was founded by tedsters including kevin kelly and stewart brand .	這是個長期基金會的計畫 , 由tedster們創立 , 包括kevinkeelly和stewart品牌 。
and what we're looking for is news stories that might still matter 50 or 100 or 10 , 000 years from now .	我們在尋找的新聞可能是50、100、100、100 , 000年後的新聞 。
and when you look at the news through that filter , a lot falls by the wayside .	當你透過過濾來看新聞時 , 許多事情會被一邊倒下 。
to take the top stories from the a . p . this last year , is this going to matter in a decade ?	為了從a.p.去年 , 最高的故事是十年後會發生什麼事嗎 ?
is this going to matter in 50 or 100 years ?	五、一百年後這會有什麼影響嗎 ?
okay , that was kind of cool .	好吧 , 那很酷 。
but the top story of this past year was the economy , and i'm just betting that , sooner or later , this particular recession is going to be old news .	但 , 去年 , 最高的故事是經濟 , 我只是在賭 , 遲早 , 這次的衰退將會是舊的消息 。
so , what kind of stories might make a difference for the future ?	所以 , 哪些故事可能對未來造成影響呢 ?
well , let's take science .	嗯 , 咱們來談科學 。
someday , little robots will go through our bloodstreams fixing things .	有一天 , 小機器人會穿過我們的血液循環 , 固定物體 。
that someday is already here if you're a mouse .	某天你已經來到這裡了 , 如果你是老鼠 。
some recent stories: nanobees zap tumors with real bee venom ; they're sending genes into the brain ; a robot they built that can crawl through the human body .	最近的一些故事:奈米粒子用真蜜毒液將基因傳送到大腦中 , 一個可以在人體上爬行的機器人 。
what about resources ? how are we going to feed nine billion people ?	那資源呢 ? 我們要如何餵飽九十億人呢 ?
we're having trouble feeding six billion today .	現今我們有六十億的難題 。
as we heard yesterday , there's over a billion people hungry .	如我們昨天聽到的 , 有超過十億人挨餓 。
britain will starve without genetically modified crops .	英國會餓死沒有基因改造的作物 。
bill gates , fortunately , has bet a billion on [agricultural] research .	幸運的是 , 比爾•蓋茲有十億人在虛擬研究上 。
what about global politics ?	全球政治呢 ?
the world's going to be very different when and if china sets the agenda , and they may .	世界將會變得非常不一樣 , 如果中國設立了這個議程 , 他們可能會 。
they've overtaken the u . s . as the world's biggest car market , they've overtaken germany as the largest exporter , and they've started doing dna tests on kids to choose their careers .	他們已經超越美國作為世界上最大的汽車市場 , 他們已經超越德國 , 成為最大的出口國 , 他們開始在孩子身上做dna檢測 , 來選擇他們的職涯 。
we're finding all kinds of ways to push back the limits of what we know .	我們在尋找各種方法 , 把我們所知的極限推回來 。
some recent discoveries: there's an ant colony from argentina that has now spread to every continent but antarctica ; there's a selfdirected robot scientist that's made a discovery soon , science may no longer need us , and life may no longer need us either ; a microbe wakes up after 120 , 000 years .	一些近來的發現:阿根廷的螞蟻蟻已經傳播到每個大陸 , 但南極洲 , 有一個自主導的機器人科學家很快就發現了 , 科學可能不再需要我們 , 生命可能已經不再需要我們了 ; 一個微生物在120 , 000年後出現 。
it seems that with or without us , life will go on .	這似乎與我們無關 , 或沒有我們 , 生命會繼續下去 。
but my pick for the top long news story of this past year was this one: water found on the moon .	但今年我選的長期新聞報導是這一個:在月球上發現水 。
makes it a lot easier to put a colony up there .	把一個蟻群放在那裡 , 讓蟻群變得更容易 。
and if nasa doesn't do it , china might , or somebody in this room might write a big check .	如果美國太空總署不這麼做 , 中國可能 , 或在這間房間裡的人可能會寫一個大支票 。
my point is this: in the long run , some news stories are more important than others .	我的重點是:長期來看 , 有些新聞故事比其他人更重要 。
planetary scientist carolyn porco shows images from the cassini voyage to saturn , focusing on its largest moon , titan , and on frozen enceladus , which seems to shoot jets of ice .	行星科學家卡羅琳•波科展示了卡西尼航行到土星的圖像 , 把焦點放在它最大的月球 , 泰坦 , 在冰冷的土衛二上 , 這似乎是用來射擊冰的射線 。
nasa , design , exploration , science , space , technology , universe , visualizations	美國太空總署、設計、探索、科學、太空技術、宇宙、視覺化的視覺化 。
carolyn porco flies us to saturn	卡羅琳•帕羅科斯讓我們在土星的土星上飛行 。
in the next 18 minutes , i'm going to take you on a journey .	接下來的十八分鐘 , 我會帶各位踏上一段旅程 。
and it's a journey that you and i have been on for many years now , and it began some 50 years ago , when humans first stepped off our planet .	這趟旅程是你我多年來一直在旅行 , 50年前 , 人類第一次離開地球時的旅程 。
and in those 50 years , not only did we literally , physically set foot on the moon , but we have dispatched robotic spacecraft to all the planets all eight of them and we have landed on asteroids , we have rendezvoused with comets , and , at this point in time , we have a spacecraft on its way to pluto , the body formerly known as a planet .	在那五十年間 , 我們不僅是真的 , 我們在月球上設定了實體飛行器 , 我們已經把機器人太空船放到八個行星上 , 我們登陸了小行星 , 我們和彗星重生 , 此時此刻 , 我們有一艘太空船 , 飛到冥王星的路上 , 前所未有的星球 。
and all of these robotic missions are part of a bigger human journey: a voyage to understand something , to get a sense of our cosmic place , to understand something of our origins , and how earth , our planet , and we , living on it , came to be .	所有這些機械式的使命都是更大的人類旅程的一部分:一趟探險 , 去了解我們的宇宙 , 去了解我們的起源 , 以及我們的地球、地球、地球、我們 , 都活在它上 。
and of all the places in the solar system that we might go to and search for answers to questions like this , there's saturn . and we have been to saturn before we visited saturn in the early 1980s but our investigations of saturn have become far more indepth in detail since the cassini spacecraft , traveling across interplanetary space for seven years , glided into orbit around saturn in the summer of 2004 , and became at that point the farthest robotic outpost that humanity had ever established around the sun .	在太陽系中的所有地方 , 我們可能去尋找這個問題的答案 , 有土星 。 我們去過土星 。 在1980年代初期 , 我們去過土星 , 但我們對土星的調查已經變得更加獨立 , 自卡西尼號太空船橫跨了星際空間七年 , 在2004年夏天 , 飛越了軌道 , 直到當時 , 人類曾經在地球上抵達過太陽的最遠距離 。
now , the saturn system is a rich planetary system .	土星系統是一個豐富的行星系統 。
it offers mystery , scientific insight and obviously splendor beyond compare , and the investigation of this system has enormous cosmic reach .	它提供了神秘、科學的洞見 , 很明顯地 , 除了相對之外 , 這項系統的調查有著巨大的宇宙性 。
in fact , just studying the rings alone , we stand to learn a lot about the discs of stars and gas that we call the spiral galaxies .	事實上 , 光是研究光環 , 我們就站在學習很多星體和氣體的圓盤 , 我們稱之為螺旋星系 。
and here's a beautiful picture of the andromeda nebula , which is our closest , largest spiral galaxy to the milky way .	這裡有一張漂亮的andromedanebula的照片 , 是我們最近的 , 最大的螺旋星系 , 到銀河系 。
and then , here's a beautiful composite of the whirlpool galaxy , taken by the hubble space telescope .	然後 , 這裡有一個美麗的組合 , 由哈伯太空望遠鏡拍攝 。
so the journey back to saturn is really part of and is also a metaphor for a much larger human voyage to understand the interconnectedness of everything around us , and also how humans fit into that picture .	所以 , 回到土星的旅程是真的的一部分 , 也是更大的人類旅程的象徵 , 來了解我們周遭的所有事物之間的關聯性 , 以及人類如何融入這張圖片 。
and it pains me that i can't tell you all that we have learned with cassini .	這讓我很痛苦 , 我無法告訴你們我們在卡西尼學到的所有東西 。
i can't show you all the beautiful pictures that we've taken in the last two and a half years , because i simply don't have the time .	我不能給你們看過去兩年半中我們拍攝過的所有美麗照片 , 因為我根本沒有時間 。
so i'm going to concentrate on two of the most exciting stories that have emerged out of this major exploratory expedition that we are conducting around saturn , and have been for the past two and a half years .	所以 , 我將要專注在兩個最令人興奮的故事中 , 出現在這個主要的探險旅程中 , 我們在土星周圍進行 , 過去兩年半 。
saturn is accompanied by a very large and diverse collection of moons .	土星是被非常大且多樣化的衛星收集所組成 。
they range in size from a few kilometers across to as big across as the u . s .	它們的大小是從幾公里長到和美國一樣大 。
most of the beautiful pictures we've taken of saturn , in fact , show saturn in accompaniment with some of its moons . here's saturn with dione , and then , here's saturn showing the rings edgeon , showing you just how vertically thin they are , with the moon enceladus .	大部分我們拍攝過土星的美麗照片 , 事實上 , 土星和它的衛星有一些月球 。 這是土星的照片 , 土星展示了環繞的邊緣 , 向你展示了它們有多薄 , 用月球的樣子 。
now , two of the 47 moons that saturn has are standouts .	現在 , 土星的四十七個衛星中有兩個是站立的 。
and those are titan and enceladus . titan is saturn's largest moon , and , until cassini had arrived there , was the largest single expanse of unexplored terrain that we had remaining in our solar system .	這些是土衛六和土衛二 。 土衛六是土星最大的月球 , 直到卡西尼抵達 , 是我們太陽系中最大的未探索的地形 。
and it is a body that has long intrigued people who've watched the planets .	它是一種身體有很長的好奇心人士 , 他們看過行星 。
it has a very large , thick atmosphere , and in fact , its surface environment was believed to be more like the environment we have here on the earth , or at least had in the past , than any other body in the solar system .	它有一個很大、很厚的大氣層 , 事實上 , 它的表面環境被認為比較像地球上的環境 , 至少過去的太陽系中任何其他身體 。
its atmosphere is largely molecular nitrogen , like you are breathing here in this room , except that its atmosphere is suffused with simple organic materials like methane and propane and ethane .	它的大氣層主要是分子氮 , 就像你在這個房間裡呼吸一樣 , 除了大氣中含有簡單的有機物質 , 如甲烷、丙烷和乙烷 。
and these molecules high up in the atmosphere of titan get broken down , and their products join together to make haze particles .	而這些分子在土衛六的大氣中高高 , 就會被破壞 , 它們的產品結合在一起 , 製造出大氣粒子 。
this haze is ubiquitous . it's completely global and enveloping titan .	這種混亂是無所不在的 , 完全是全球化的 , 並且將土衛六加入 。
and that's why you cannot see down to the surface with our eyes in the visible region of the spectrum .	這就是為什麼你無法在光譜的可見區域看到表面 。
but these haze particles , it was surmised , before we got there with cassini , over billions and billions of years , gently drifted down to the surface and coated the surface in a thick organic sludge .	但這些巨大的粒子被推斷 , 在我們和casssini一起到達之前 , 數十億年來 , 輕輕地向下漂移到表面 , 並在厚的有機河中覆蓋了表面 。
so like the equivalent , the titan equivalent , of tar , or oil , or what we didn't know what .	像泰坦一樣 , 泰坦和油 , 或石油 , 或我們不知道什麼 。
but this is what we suspected . and these molecules , especially methane and ethane , can be liquids at the surface temperatures of titan .	但這是我們懷疑的 。 這些分子 , 尤其是甲烷和乙烷 , 在土衛六的表面溫度上是液體 。
and so it turns out that methane is to titan what water is to the earth .	結果發現 , 甲烷就是土衛六 , 水對地球的意義 。
it's a condensable in the atmosphere , and so recognizing this circumstance brought to the fore a whole world of bizarre possibilities . you can have methane clouds , ok , and above those clouds , you have this hundreds of kilometers of haze , which prevent any sunlight from getting to the surface .	在大氣中 , 它是可以穿透的 , 並且承認這個環境會造成整個奇怪的可能性 。 你可以有甲烷雲 , 在這些雲上 , 你有數百公里的哈西 , 可以預防任何太陽光到達表面 。
the temperature at the surface is some 350 degrees below zero fahrenheit .	表面的溫度低於華氏零度的350度 。
but despite that cold , you could have rain falling down on the surface of titan .	儘管如此冷 , 土衛六的表面仍有降雨量 。
and doing on titan what rain does on the earth: it carves gullies ; it forms rivers and cataracts ; it can create canyons ; it can pool in large basins and craters .	在土衛六上 , 下雨是怎麼做的 , 它會雕刻猜測 ; 它會形成河流和白馬 , 它能創造峽谷 ; 它能在大盆地和坑中流動 。
it can wash the sludge off high mountain peaks and hills , down into the lowlands . so stop and think for a minute .	它可以把垃圾從高山山丘和山丘脫落到低地上 。 所以停下來 , 思考一下 。
try to imagine what the surface of titan might look like .	試想一下泰坦的表面會是什麼樣子 。
it's dark . high noon on titan is as dark as deep earth twilight on the earth .	它是黑暗的 , 在土衛六上午的黑暗和地球的深光一樣 。
it's cold , it's eerie , it's misty , it might be raining , and you might be standing on the shores of lake michigan brimming with paint thinner .	很冷 , 很噁心 , 很糟糕 , 可能會下雨 , 你可能會站在密西根湖的邊緣 , 用油漆薄的薄膜 。
that is the view that we had of the surface of titan before we got there with cassini , and i can tell you that what we have found on titan , though it is not the same in detail , is every bit as fascinating as that story is .	這是我們在泰坦的表面之前所看到的景象 , 是我們和卡西尼一起到達的 , 我可以告訴各位 , 我們在泰坦所發現的 , 雖然細節不一樣 , 每一點都和故事的吸引力一樣 。
and for us , it has been like the cassini people it has been like a jules verne adventure come true .	對我們來說 , 它就像是卡西尼人 , 它就像是一場朱爾文的冒險 。
as i said , it has a thick , extensive atmosphere .	如我所說 , 它的大氣層很厚 , 很大 。
this is a picture of titan , backlit by the sun , with the rings as a beautiful backdrop .	這是土衛六的照片 , 太陽的背景 , 光環是美麗的背景 。
and yet another moon there i don't even know which one it is . it's a very extensive atmosphere .	另外一個月亮 , 我甚至不知道它是哪一個 。 這是個非常廣泛的大氣層 。
we have instruments on cassini which can see down to the surface through this atmosphere , and my camera system is one of them .	我們有卡西尼號的儀器 , 可以透過這個大氣層看到表面 , 我的攝影系統是其中之一 。
and we have taken pictures like this .	我們拍了像這樣的照片 。
and what you see is bright and dark regions , and that's about as far as it got for us .	你看到的是明亮和黑暗的區域 , 正是它為我們帶來的程度 。
it was so mystifying: we couldn't make out what we were seeing on titan .	這非常神秘:我們無法弄清楚我們在土衛六上所看到的 。
when you look closer at this region , you start to see things like sinuous channels we didn't know . you see a few round things .	當你仔細觀察這個區域 , 你就會開始看到一些我們不知道的東西 。 你可以看到一些圓形的東西 。
this , we later found out , is , in fact , a crater , but there are very few craters on the surface of titan , meaning it's a very young surface .	後來我們發現 , 事實上 , 一個坑 , 但土衛六表面上有很少的坑 , 意思是 , 它是非常年輕的表面 。
and there are features that look tectonic .	有些特徵看起來是電子的 。
they look like they've been pulled apart .	它們看起來就像是被拉開的一樣 。
whenever you see anything linear on a planet , it means there's been a fracture , like a fault .	每當你在星球上看到任何線性的東西 , 就會有裂痕 , 例如一個斷層 。
and so it's been tectonically altered .	所以它已經有了相同的改變 。
but we couldn't make sense of our images , until , six months after we got into orbit , an event occurred that many have regarded as the highlight of cassini's investigation of titan .	但我們無法理解我們的影像 , 直到我們進入軌道六個月後 , 發生了一場事件 , 許多事件被認為是卡西尼對泰坦的調查 。
and that was the deployment of the huygens probe , the europeanbuilt huygens probe that cassini had carried for seven years across the solar system . we deployed it to the atmosphere of titan , it took two and a half hours to descend , and it landed on the surface .	這是胡布斯探測器的部署 , 歐洲builthugensini已經在太陽系中運行了七年 。 我們將它部署到土衛六的大氣層 , 花了兩個半小時 , 才能抵達地表 。
and i just want to emphasize how significant an event this is .	我只想強調這個事件有多重要 。
this is a device of human making , and it landed in the outer solar system for the first time in human history .	這是人類製造的裝置 , 它在人類歷史上第一次登陸太陽系 。
it is so significant that , in my mind , this was an event that should have been celebrated with ticker tape parades in every city across the u . s . and europe , and sadly , that wasn't the case .	在我看來 , 這件事非常重要 , 應該要在美國和歐洲的每個城市都要慶祝這個遊行 , 很遺憾的是 , 這並非如此 。
it was significant for another reason . this is an international mission , and this event was celebrated in europe , in germany , and the celebratory presentations were given in english accents , and american accents , and german accents , and french and italian and dutch accents .	這很重要 , 原因是 , 這是國際性的使命 , 而這個事件在歐洲被慶祝 , 在德國 , 慶祝的簡報是英文 , 美國口音 , 德語 , 法國和義大利語和荷蘭口音 。
it was a moving demonstration of what the words " united nations " are supposed to mean: a true union of nations joined together in a colossal effort for good .	它是關於 「 聯合國 」 這個詞的移動示範 , 本來應該是:一個真正的國家加入一個很大的努力 。
and , in this case , it was a massive undertaking to explore a planet , and to come to understand a planetary system that , for all of human history , had been unreachable , and now humans had actually touched it .	在這個例子中 , 它是一個巨大的探索一個星球 , 為了所有人類歷史 , 人類的歷史 , 一直是不可思議的 , 現在人類已經觸動了這個星球 。
so it was i mean , i'm getting goose bumps just talking about it .	所以 , 我的意思是 , 我得到了鵝凸起 , 只是談到它 。
it was a tremendously emotional event , and it's something that i will personally never forget , and you shouldn't either .	那是個非常感情的事件 , 我個人永遠不會忘記 , 你也不該忘記 。
but anyway , the probe took measurements of the atmosphere on the way down , and it also took panoramic pictures .	總之 , 探測器採用了大氣層下降的測量 , 同時也拍了全景的照片 。
and i can't tell you what it was like to see the first pictures of titan's surface from the probe . and this is what we saw .	我不能告訴你們泰坦的第一張圖片是泰坦的表面 。 這是我們所看到的 。
and it was a shocker , because it was everything we wanted those other pictures taken from orbit to be .	這很震驚 , 因為那是我們想要的其他照片從軌道拍攝到的一切 。
it was an unambiguous pattern , a geological pattern .	它是一個無所不在的圖案 , 一個地質圖案 。
it's a dendritic drainage pattern that can be formed only by the flow of liquids .	它是種垂直的排放模式 , 只能通過液體的流動來形成 。
and you can follow these channels and you can see how they all converge .	你可以追蹤這些頻道 , 看看它們如何被轉換 。
and they converge into this channel here , which drains into this region .	然後他們把這些通道轉換成這個區域 ,
you are looking at a shoreline .	你看到的是海岸線 。
was this a shoreline of fluids ? we didn't know .	這是流體的海岸線嗎 ? 我們不知道 。
but this is somewhat of a shoreline .	但這有點像海岸線 。
this picture is taken at 16 kilometers .	這張照片是16公里拍攝的 。
this is the picture taken at eight kilometers , ok ? again , the shoreline .	這張照片是8公里拍的 , 好嗎 ? 再次是海岸線 。
okay , now , 16 kilometers , eight kilometers this is roughly an airline altitude .	好 , 現在 , 16公里 , 8公里 , 大約是航空高度 。
if you were going to take an airplane trip across the u . s . , you would be flying at these altitudes .	如果你要飛越美國的飛機旅行 , 你會在這些高度飛行 。
so , this is the picture you would have at the window of titanian airlines as you fly across the surface of titan .	這是你在鐵達尼亞航空公司的窗邊 , 飛越泰坦的表面 。
and then finally , the probe came to rest on the surface , and i'm going to show you , ladies and gentlemen , the first picture ever taken from the surface of a moon in the outer solar system .	最後 , 探測器在表面休息了 , 我要給大家看 , 各位先生女士 , 第一張從外太陽系的表面拍攝的照片 。
and here is the horizon , ok ?	這是地平線 , 好嗎 ?
these are probably water ice pebbles , yes ?	這些可能是冰泡 , 是吧 ?
and obviously , it landed in one of these flat , dark regions and it didn't sink out of sight . so it wasn't fluid that we landed in .	很顯然 , 它落在一個平坦、黑暗的區域 , 且它沒有從視線下沉 。 所以它不是我們降落的液體 。
what the probe came down in was basically the titan equivalent of a mud flat .	基本上 , 探測器下降的 , 基本上是泰坦的平面 。
this is an unconsolidated ground that is suffused with liquid methane .	這是一個與液態甲烷混合的土地 。
and it's probably the case that this material has washed off the highlands of titan through these channels that we saw , and has drained over billions of years to fill in lowlying basins .	可能是這種材料在我們看到的這些通道中已經被沖掉了 , 數十億年以來 , 以便填滿低沉的盆地 。
and that is what the huygens probe landed in .	這就是huygens探針登陸的原因 。
but still , there was no sign in our images , or even in the huygens' images , of any large , open bodies of fluids .	但是 , 我們的影像中仍然沒有任何跡象 , 甚至在huygens的圖片中 , 任何大型開放的液體 。
where were they ? it got even more puzzling when we found dunes .	他們在哪裡 ? 當我們發現沙丘時 , 會更加困惑 。
ok , so this is our movie of the equatorial region of titan , showing these dunes . these are dunes that are 100 meters tall , separated by a few kilometers , and they go on for miles and miles and miles .	好 , 這是我們在土衛六的赤道地區的電影 , 展示這些沙丘 。 這些沙丘是一百公尺高 , 被幾公里分開的沙丘 , 經過了數英里、數英哩、數英哩 。
there's hundreds , up to a 1 , 000 or 1 , 200 miles of dunes .	有數百英哩高達1000或1200英哩的沙丘 。
this is the saharan desert of titan .	這是泰坦的撒哈拉沙漠 。
it's obviously a place which is very dry , or you wouldn't get dunes .	很明顯地 , 一個非常乾燥的地方 , 或者你不會得到沙丘 。
so again , it got puzzling that there were no bodies of fluid , until finally , we saw lakes in the polar regions .	同樣的 , 它變得令人困惑 , 沒有任何液體 , 直到最後 , 我們看到了北極地區的湖泊 。
and there is a lake scene in the south polar region of titan .	土衛六的南極地區有一個湖 。
it's about the size of lake ontario .	大小和安大略湖差不多 。
and then , only a week and a half ago , we flew over the north pole of titan and found , again , we found a feature here the size of the caspian sea .	直到一週半前 , 我們飛越北極 , 再次發現 , 我們發現一個特徵 , 大小是caspian海 。
so it seems that the liquids , for some reason we don't understand , or during at least this season , are apparently at the poles of titan .	所以看來 , 液體 , 基於某些我們不了解的原因 , 或至少在這個季節 , 顯然是在泰坦的極端 。
and i think you would agree that we have found titan is a remarkable , mystical place . it's exotic , it's alien , but yet strangely earthlike , and having earthlike geological formations and a tremendous geographical diversity , and is a fascinating world whose only rival in the solar system for complexity and richness is the earth itself .	我想你會同意 , 我們發現泰坦是很神秘的 , 很奇怪 , 它是外星人 , 但卻是奇怪的地球 , 有著類似地球的地質形 , 和一個巨大的地質多樣性 , 一個令人著迷的世界 , 只有在太陽系中 , 足夠的和豐富 , 才是地球本身 。
and so now we go onto enceladus . enceladus is a small moon , it's about a tenth the size of titan . and you can see it here next to england , just to show you the size . this is not meant to be a threat .	所以現在我們去了土衛二 。 土衛二是一個小的衛星 , 它大概是土衛六的十分之一 。 你可以看到它在英格蘭旁邊 , 讓你看到它的大小 。 這不是威脅 。
and enceladus is very white , it's very bright , and its surface is obviously wrecked with fractures .	土衛二是非常白的 , 非常明亮 , 它的表面顯然是破碎的 。
it is a very geologically active body .	它是一個非常活躍的身體 。
but the mother lode of discoveries on enceladus was found at the south pole and we're looking at the south pole here where we found this system of fractures .	但土衛二的發現是南極的發現 , 我們現在看到的是南極 , 在那裡我們找到了這個碎片的系統 。
and they're a different color because they're a different composition .	它們是不同的顏色 , 因為它們是不同的組成 。
they are coated . these fractures are coated with organic materials .	它們是複製的 。 這些碎片和有機物質結合在一起 。
moreover , this whole , entire region , the south polar region , has elevated temperatures . it's the hottest place on the planet , on the body .	此外 , 整個地區 , 南極地區的溫度升高了 。 它是地球上最熱的地方 , 位在人體上 。
that's as bizarre as finding that the antarctic on the earth is hotter than the tropics .	這就像是發現地球上的南極比熱帶更熱一樣 。
and then , when we took additional pictures , we discovered that from these fractures are issuing jets of fine , icy particles extending hundreds of miles into space .	然後 , 當我們拍下額外的圖片 , 我們發現 , 從這些碎片中 , 噴射出好的 , 冰粒會延伸數百英里的空間 。
and when we colorcode this image , to bring out the faint light levels , we see that these jets feed a plume that , in fact , we see , in other images , goes thousands of miles into the space above enceladus .	當我們把這張影像編碼出來 , 把微弱的光線帶出來 , 我們會發現 , 這些噴射器會餵飽一大堆 , 事實上 , 在其他的影像中 , 會在土衛二上數千英里進入太空 。
my team and i have examined images like this , and like this one , and have thought about the other results from cassini .	我和我的團隊檢查了像這樣的影像 , 就像這張 , 從卡西尼尼州開始思考其他的結果 。
and we have arrived at the conclusion that these jets may be erupting from pockets of liquid water under the surface of enceladus .	我們的結論是 , 這些噴射機可能從土衛二表面下噴出液態水 。
so we have , possibly , liquid water , organic materials and excess heat .	所以 , 我們可能有液態水、有機物質和過多的熱能 。
in other words , we have possibly stumbled upon the holy grail of modern day planetary exploration , or in other words , an environment that is potentially suitable for living organisms .	換句話說 , 我們已經發現了現代地球探索的聖杯 , 換句話說 , 一個可能適合生物的環境 。
and i don't think i need to tell you that the discovery of life elsewhere in our solar system , whether it be on enceladus or elsewhere , would have enormous cultural and scientific implications .	我不認為我需要告訴各位 , 在我們的太陽系中發現了生命 , 不論是在土衛二或其他地方 , 都會有巨大的文化和科學影響 。
because if we could demonstrate that genesis had occurred not once , but twice , independently , in our solar system , then that means , by inference , it has occurred a staggering number of times throughout the universe and its 13 . 7 billion year history .	因為如果我們能證明遺傳基因不只發生一次 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 獨立兩次 , 那就表示 , 根據推論 , 它在整個宇宙中發生了數次驚人的數量 , 且它137億年的歷史 。
right now , earth is the only planet still that we know is teeming with life .	目前 , 地球是唯一一個我們知道的行星 , 存在於生命中 。
it is precious , it is unique , it is still , so far , the only home we've ever known .	它很珍貴 , 它是獨一無二的 , 到目前為止 , 我們唯一認識的家 。
and if any of you were alert and coherent during the 1960s and we'd forgive you , if you weren't , ok you would remember this very famous picture taken by the apollo 8 astronauts in 1968 .	如果你們當中有人在1960年代警覺和協調 , 我們會原諒你 , 如果你不是 , 還記得1968年阿波羅8號太空人拍的這張著名的照片 。
it was the first time that earth was imaged from space , and it had an enormous impact on our sense of place in the universe , and our sense of responsibility for the protection of our own planet .	那是第一次 , 地球是從太空中拍攝的 , 它對我們在宇宙中的位置有著巨大的影響 , 以及我們對地球保護的責任感 。
well , we on cassini have taken an equivalent first , a picture that no human eye has ever seen before .	嗯 , 我們在卡西尼拍了一張相同的第一張照片 , 沒有人眼見過的照片 。
it is a total eclipse of the sun , seen from the other side of saturn .	它是土星另一端的日蝕 , 從土星的角度看 。
and in this impossibly beautiful picture , you see the main rings backlit by the sun , you see the refracted image of the sun and you see this ring created , in fact , by the exhalations of enceladus .	在這張可能是美麗的圖片中 , 你可以看到太陽的主要環繞著背景 , 你可以看到太陽重新定義的形象 , 事實上 , 這個環是由土衛二所產生的 。
but as if that weren't brilliant enough , we can spot , in this beautiful image , sight of our own planet , cradled in the arms of saturn's rings .	但 , 彷彿那還不夠聰明 , 我們可以在這個美麗的圖像中 , 看到我們自己的星球 , 在土星環的手臂中擠壓 。
now , there is something deeply moving about seeing ourselves from afar , and capturing the sight of our little , blueocean planet in the skies of other worlds .	現在 , 有一個深深的感動 , 關於我們自己從遠處看到 , 捕捉到我們在其他世界的小藍綠色的行星 。
and that , and the perspective of ourselves that we gain from that , may be , in the end , the finest reward that we earn from this journey of discovery that started half a century ago .	而我們從中得到的這個觀點 , 可能是 , 最終 , 我們從這個發現的最好的獎勵 , 從半個世紀前就得到 。
as of 2005 , only 15 percent of the world was mapped . this slows the delivery of aid after a disaster and hides the economic potential of unused lands and unknown roads . in this short talk , google's lalitesh katragadda demos map maker , a group mapmaking tool that people around the globe are using to map their world .	到了2005年 , 世界上只有15%是被繪製出來的 。 這種減緩了災難後的援助 , 隱藏了未知的土地和未知的道路 。 在短篇演說中 , 谷歌的卡達加達•德摩爾 , 一個全球各地居民使用地地地地地地地地地地地圖工具 , 用地圖來繪製他們的世界 。
collaboration , design , map , technology	合作 , 設計 , 地圖 , 科技 , 科技 。
lalitesh katragadda: making maps to fight disaster , build economies	laliteshkatragada:繪製對抗災難的地圖 , 建立經濟體 。
in 2008 , cyclone nargis devastated myanmar .	在2008年 , 居魯士納基人摧毀了緬甸人 。
millions of people were in severe need of help .	數百萬人有嚴重的幫助 。
the u . n . wanted to rush people and supplies to the area .	聯合國想要把人和供應給給當地 。
but there were no maps , no maps of roads , no maps showing hospitals , no way for help to reach the cyclone victims .	但沒有地圖 , 沒有道路地圖 , 沒有地圖顯示醫院 , 無法協助到達cyclone受害者 。
when we look at a map of los angeles or london , it is hard to believe that as of 2005 , only 15 percent of the world was mapped to a geocodable level of detail .	當我們看到洛杉磯或倫敦的地圖時 , 很難相信在2005年 , 世界上只有15%的人口被繪製成可數量的細節 。
the u . n . ran headfirst into a problem that the majority of the world's populous faces: not having detailed maps .	聯合國為世上大部分人面臨的難題:沒有詳細的地圖 。
but help was coming .	但 , 協助已經來了 。
at google , 40 volunteers used a new software to map 120 , 000 kilometers of roads , 3 , 000 hospitals , logistics and relief points .	在google , 40個志願者用一個新的軟體來繪製十二萬公里的道路 , 三千間醫院、物流和救援點 。
and it took them four days .	他們花了四天 。
the new software they used ? google mapmaker .	他們使用的新軟體 ? 谷歌地圖製造者 。
google mapmaker is a technology that empowers each of us to map what we know locally .	google地圖製造者是一項科技 , 讓我們每個人都能夠繪製我們所知的地圖 。
people have used this software to map everything from roads to rivers , from schools to local businesses , and video stores to the corner store .	人們用這個軟體來繪製所有東西 , 從路到河流 , 從學校到當地的企業 , 視頻店到角落商店 。
nobel prize nominee hernando de soto recognized that the key to economic liftoff for most developing countries is to tap the vast amounts of uncapitalized land .	諾貝爾獎提名赫南多•索托認為對大部分開發中國家的經濟利益的關鍵是把大量未受控制的土地 。
for example , a trillion dollars of real estate remains uncapitalized in india alone .	舉例來說 , 僅在印度 , 一兆美元的房地產仍未被排除 。
in the last year alone , thousands of users in 170 countries have mapped millions of pieces of information , and created a map of a level of detail never thought viable .	光是去年 , 十七個國家就有數以百萬計的使用者 , 創造出一個細節的地圖 , 從來沒有想過可行 。
and this was made possible by the power of passionate users everywhere .	以熱情使用者的力量實現了 。
let's look at some of the maps being created by users right now .	現在我們來看看一些使用者的地圖 。
so , as we speak , people are mapping the world in these 170 countries .	所以 , 如同我們所說的 , 在這個170個國家中 , 人們在繪製這個世界 。
you can see bridget in africa who just mapped a road in senegal .	你可以看到非洲的橋 , 剛在塞內加爾畫了一條路 。
and , closer to home , chalua , an n . g . road in bangalore .	然後 , 靠近夏盧亞 , 一個n.g.g.g.g , 在班加羅爾 。
this is the result of computational geometry , gesture recognition , and machine learning .	這是計算幾何學的結果 , 手勢辨識 , 以及機器學習 。
this is a victory of thousands of users , in hundreds of cities , one user , one edit at a time .	這是一場勝利 , 數百個城市 , 一個使用者 , 一次編輯 。
this is an invitation to the 70 percent of our unmapped planet .	這是我們70%未開發的地球的邀請 。
welcome to the new world .	歡迎來到新的世界 。
in 2003 , the palestinian village of budrus mounted a 10monthlong nonviolent protest to stop a barrier being built across their olive groves . did you hear about it ? didn't think so . brazilian filmmaker julia bacha asks why we only pay attention to violence in the israelpalestine conflict and not to the nonviolent leaders who may one day bring peace .	在2003年 , 布德魯斯的巴勒斯坦村落在十個月長的非暴力抗議中 , 阻止一個障礙在他們的橄欖球之中 。 你聽說過嗎 ? 不這麼想 。 巴西的電影製片工程師朱利亞.朱利亞問我們為什麼只關注以色列的戰爭衝突 , 而非暴力的領袖 , 不關注那些可能帶來和平的非暴力領導者 。
arts , communication , compassion , entertainment , film , peace , violence , war	藝術、溝通、同情、娛樂、電影、和平、暴力、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭 。
julia bacha: pay attention to nonviolence	朱麗亞:請注意非暴力的非暴力行為 。
for the last 8 years , i have dedicated my life to documenting the work of israelis and palestinians who are trying to end the conflict using peaceful means .	過去8年來 , 我致力於記錄以色列和巴勒斯坦人的作品 , 他們試圖用和平的方式來結束衝突 。
when i travel with my work across europe and the united states , one question always comes up: where is the palestinian gandhi ?	當我在歐洲和美國的研究中旅行時 , 有一個問題總是出現:巴勒斯坦甘地在哪裡 ?
why aren't palestinians using nonviolent resistance ?	為什麼巴勒斯坦人不使用非暴力抗爭 ?
the challenge i face when i hear this question is that often i have just returned from the middle east where i spent my time filming dozens of palestinians who are using nonviolence to defend their lands and water resources from israeli soldiers and settlers .	當我聽到這個問題時 , 我所面臨的挑戰是 , 通常我剛從中東返回 , 我花了很多時間拍攝數十位巴勒斯坦人 , 他們用非暴力的方式來保護他們的土地和水資源 , 以色列士兵和移民者 。
these leaders are trying to forge a massive national nonviolent movement to end the occupation and build peace in the region .	這些領導人正試著要為一個大規模的全國非暴力運動來終結職業 , 並在這個地區建立和平 。
yet , most of you have probably never heard about them .	然而 , 大部分的人可能從來沒有聽過他們 。
this divide between what's happening on the ground and perceptions abroad is one of the key reasons why we don't have yet a palestinian peaceful resistance movement that has been successful .	這種差異在地面和國外感知的差異之處在於我們尚未完成巴勒斯坦和平抗爭運動的關鍵原因之一 。
so i'm here today to talk about the power of attention , the power of your attention , and the emergence and development of nonviolent movements in the west bank , gaza and elsewhere but today , my case study is going to be palestine .	所以今天我來到這裡 , 要談注意力的力量 , 你的注意力 , 以及在西銀行、加薩和其他地方的非暴力運動的崛起和發展 。 但今天 , 我的案例研究將會是巴勒斯坦 。
i believe that what's mostly missing for nonviolence to grow is not for palestinians to start adopting nonviolence , but for us to start paying attention to those who already are .	我相信 , 成長過程中大部分缺少的非暴力 , 並不是為了要讓巴勒斯坦人開始採用非暴力 , 而是要我們開始注意那些已經被關注的人 。
allow me to illustrate this point by taking you to this village called budrus .	讓我來說明一下這一點 , 帶你去這個叫做布德魯斯的村莊 。
about seven years ago , they faced extinction , because israel announced it would build a separation barrier , and part of this barrier would be built on top of the village .	大約七年前 , 他們面臨絕種 , 因為以色列宣佈它會建立一個分離障礙 , 部分的障礙會在村莊頂端 。
they would lose 40 percent of their land and be surrounded , so they would lose free access to the rest of the west bank .	他們會失去百分之四十的土地 , 被圍繞 , 所以他們會失去自由取得西岸的其他地方 。
through inspired local leadership , they launched a peaceful resistance campaign to stop that from happening .	透過當地的領導力 , 他們發起了一種和平的抗拒運動 , 來阻止它發生 。
let me show you some brief clips , so you have a sense for what that actually looked like on the ground .	讓我給你們看一些簡短的片段 , 所以你有感覺到它在地面上實際的樣子 。
palestinian woman: we were told the wall would separate palestine from israel .	巴勒斯坦女子:我們被告知牆會和以色列分開巴勒斯坦 。
here in budrus , we realized the wall would steal our land .	在布德魯斯 , 我們了解到牆會偷走我們的土地 。
israeli man: the fence has , in fact , created a solution to terror .	以色列人:事實上 , 圍籬已經創造出了對恐怖的解決方案 。
man: today you're invited to a peaceful march .	男子:今天你被邀請去和平遊行 。
you are joined by dozens of your israeli brothers and sisters .	你被數十位以色列兄弟姐妹加入 。
israeli activist: nothing scares the army more than nonviolent opposition .	以色列行動主義者:軍隊比非暴力的反對者更害怕 。
woman: we saw the men trying to push the soldiers , but none of them could do that .	女子:我們看到男人試圖推動士兵 , 但他們都無法做到 。
but i think the girls could do it .	但我認為 , 女孩們可以做到 。
fatah party member: we must empty our minds of traditional thinking .	fatah黨員:我們必須清空我們對傳統思維的思想 。
hamas party member: we were in complete harmony , and we wanted to spread it to all of palestine .	哈馬斯派對成員:我們在完全和諧 , 我們想要把它傳播給所有巴勒斯坦 。
chanting: one united nation .	湯:一個聯合國 。
fatah , hamas and the popular front !	fatah , 哈馬斯和受歡迎的前面 !
news anchor: the clashes over the fence continue .	新聞主持人:圍籬的衝擊持續著 。
reporter: israeli border police were sent to disperse the crowd .	記者:以色列邊境警察被送去散播群眾 。
they were allowed to use any force necessary .	他們被允許使用任何必要的力量 。
man: these are live bullets .	男子:這些是活子彈 。
it's like fallujah . shooting everywhere .	這就像是 「 四處槍擊 」 一樣 。
israeli activist: i was sure we were all going to die .	以色列行動主義者:我相信我們都要死 。
but there were others around me who weren't even cowering .	但我身邊還有一些人 , 他們甚至沒有在作戰 。
israeli soldier: a nonviolent protest is not going to stop the [unclear] .	以色列士兵:非暴力抗議不會阻止這場戰爭 。
protester: this is a peaceful march .	提斯特:這是一個和平的遊行 。
there is no need to use violence .	不需要使用暴力 。
chanting: we can do it ! we can do it !	湯姆:我們能做到 ! 我們能做到 !
julia bacha: when i first heard about the story of budrus , i was surprised that the international media had failed to cover the extraordinary set of events that happened seven years ago , in 2003 .	朱麗亞.巴赫亞:當我第一次聽到布德魯斯的故事時 , 我很驚訝國際媒體並沒有報導七年前發生的非凡事件 , 在2003年 。
what was even more surprising was the fact that budrus was successful .	更令人驚訝的是 , 布德魯斯成功了 。
the residents , after 10 months of peaceful resistance , convinced the israeli government to move the route of the barrier off their lands and to the green line , which is the internationally recognized boundary between israel and the palestinian territories .	居民 , 在十個月的和平抗爭之後 , 說服了以色列政府把屏障從他們的土地移到綠線 , 也就是國際認可以色列和巴勒斯坦領土之間的界線 。
the resistance in budrus has since spread to villages across the west bank and to palestinian neighborhoods in jerusalem .	布德魯斯的抗藥性從西岸散播到村落 , 到耶路撒冷的巴勒斯坦社區 。
yet the media remains mostly silent on these stories .	然而 , 媒體仍然沉默在這些故事中 。
this silence carries profound consequences for the likelihood that nonviolence can grow , or even survive , in palestine .	這種沉默對非暴力的可能造成很深的影響 , 甚至在巴勒斯坦 , 會造成深遠的影響 。
violent resistance and nonviolent resistance share one very important thing in common ; they are both a form of theater seeking an audience to their cause .	暴力的抵抗力和非暴力抗爭 , 共通性非常重要 ; 它們兩種形式都是尋求觀眾的成因 。
if violent actors are the only ones constantly getting frontpage covers and attracting international attention to the palestinian issue , it becomes very hard for nonviolent leaders to make the case to their communities that civil disobedience is a viable option in addressing their plight .	如果暴力的演員是唯一經常收到的封面 , 吸引國際對巴勒斯坦議題的注意 , 那對非暴力領袖來說 , 公民不服從的社區來說是可行的 。
the power of attention is probably going to come as no surprise to the parents in the room .	注意力的力量可能是房間裡的父母不會感到驚訝 。
the surest way to make your child throw increasingly louder tantrums is by giving him attention the first time he throws a fit .	要讓你的孩子更大聲地丟棄幻肢的確切方法 , 就是首次給他注意他丟了一套套套裝置 。
the tantrum will become what childhood psychologists call a functional behavior , since the child has learned that he can get parental attention out of it .	抗病毒會變成兒童心理學家稱之為 「 功能性行為 」 , 因為小孩子已經學到 , 他可以從中得到父母的注意力 。
parents can incentivize or disincentivize behavior simply by giving or withdrawing attention to their children .	父母可以獎勵或不獎勵行為 , 只透過給予或給予孩子注意 。
but that's true for adults too .	但對成年人來說也是如此 。
in fact , the behavior of entire communities and countries can be influenced , depending on where the international community chooses to focus its attention .	事實上 , 整個社區和國家的行為可能會受到影響 , 取決於國際社會選擇集中注意力的地方 。
i believe that at the core of ending the conflict in the middle east and bringing peace is for us to transform nonviolence into a functional behavior by giving a lot more attention to the nonviolent leaders on the ground today .	我相信 , 在中東結束衝突的核心 , 並且帶來和平 , 是為了我們把非暴力行為轉變成功能性行為 , 讓現今地面上非暴力領導者更關注 。
in the course of taking my film to villages in the west bank , in gaza and in east jerusalem , i have seen the impact that even one documentary film can have in influencing the transformation .	在拍攝我的影片到西岸的村落、加薩、東耶路撒冷的村落裡 , 我看過即使一部紀錄片也能影響改造 。
in a village called wallajeh , which sits very close to jerusalem , the community was facing a very similar plight to budrus .	在一個叫瓦拉賈的村落 , 非常接近耶路撒冷 , 這個社區正面臨著類似的佛祖 。
they were going to be surrounded , lose a lot of their lands and not have freedom of access , either to the west bank or jerusalem .	他們會被圍繞著 , 失去了很多土地 , 卻沒有自由取得 , 不論是西岸或耶路撒冷 。
they had been using nonviolence for about two years but had grown disenchanted since nobody was paying attention .	他們已經使用非暴力手段兩年了 , 但從沒人注意到 , 他們已經漸漸消失了 。
so we organized a screening .	所以我們組織了一個篩檢 。
a week later , they held the most wellattended and disciplined demonstration to date .	一個禮拜後 , 他們舉辦了最完整、最具體的示範給日期看 。
the organizers say that the villagers , upon seeing the story of budrus documented in a film , felt that there were indeed people following what they were doing , that people cared .	組織者說 , 村民在電影中看到布德魯斯的故事 , 真的有人跟著他們在做什麽 , 人們在乎的事 。
so they kept on going .	所以他們繼續走下去 。
on the israeli side , there is a new peace movement called solidariot , which means solidarity in hebrew .	以色列的一面 , 有一個新的和平運動 , 叫做索里德里特 , 意思是希伯來語的團結 。
the leaders of this movement have been using budrus as one of their primary recruiting tools .	這個運動的領導人 , 一直在用布德魯斯作為他們主要的招募工具之一 。
they report that israelis who had never been active before , upon seeing the film , understand the power of nonviolence and start joining their activities .	他們報告說 , 以色列人從來沒有活躍 , 在看電影時 , 了解非暴力的力量 , 開始加入他們的活動 。
the examples of wallajeh and the solidariot movement show that even a smallbudget independent film can play a role in transforming nonviolence into a functional behavior .	瓦哈和索里達運動的例子顯示 , 即使是小型的獨立電影 , 也可以扮演非暴力行為的角色 。
now imagine the power that big media players could have if they started covering the weekly nonviolent demonstrations happening in villages like bil'in , ni'lin , wallajeh , in jerusalem neighborhoods like sheikh jarrah and silwan the nonviolent leaders would become more visible , valued and effective in their work .	想像一下 , 大型媒體玩家能擁有的力量如果他們開始報導每週的非暴力示威 , 例如bilin、ni''''''lin、瓦拉賈 , 在耶路撒冷的鄰里中 , 像sikhjarrah和silwan這樣的非暴力領袖 , 會變得更可見、更有價值、更有效率 , 更有效率 。
i believe that the most important thing is to understand that if we don't pay attention to these efforts , they are invisible , and it's as if they never happened .	我相信 , 最重要的是 , 如果我們不注意這些努力 , 它們是隱形的 , 就好像從未發生過一樣 。
but i have seen first hand that if we do , they will multiply .	但我首先看過如果我們做的話 , 它們會乘以乘法 。
if they multiply , their influence will grow in the overall israelipalestinian conflict .	如果他們再乘上 , 他們的影響會在以色列的戰爭中成長 。
and theirs is the kind of influence that can finally unblock the situation .	而他們的影響力 , 終於可以解開這種情況 。
these leaders have proven that nonviolence works in places like budrus .	這些領袖已經證明了非暴力在像布德魯斯這樣的地方工作 。
let's give them attention so they can prove it works everywhere .	讓我們把注意力給大家 , 讓他們可以證明它無所不在 。
simon sinek has a simple but powerful model for inspirational leadership all starting with a golden circle and the question " why ? " his examples include apple , martin luther king , and the wright brothers . . .	西蒙•海克有一個簡單且強大的靈感領導模式 , 始於黃金圓圈 , 以及 「 為什麼 ? 」 他的例子包括蘋果、馬丁•路德•金和萊特兄弟......
bullseye , business , entrepreneur , leadership , sales , selling , success	子孫、企業家、企業家、領導力、銷售、銷售、成功、成功、成功 。
simon sinek: how great leaders inspire action	西蒙•薩恩克:偉大的領導人如何啟發行動 。
how do you explain when things don't go as we assume ?	你要如何解釋當事情不像我們假設的那樣發生 ?
or better , how do you explain when others are able to achieve things that seem to defy all of the assumptions ?	或更好的 , 你要如何解釋當其他人能夠達成似乎違反所有假設時 ?
for example: why is apple so innovative ?	例如:為什麼蘋果這麼創新 ?
year after year , after year , after year , they're more innovative than all their competition .	年復一年 , 年復一年 , 他們比所有的競爭者都更有創意 。
and yet , they're just a computer company .	然而 , 他們只是一家電腦公司 。
they're just like everyone else .	它們和其他人一樣 。
they have the same access to the same talent , the same agencies , the same consultants , the same media .	他們有相同的能力 , 同一個機構 , 同一個顧問 , 同一個媒體 。
then why is it that they seem to have something different ?	那麼 , 為什麼他們似乎有不同的想法 ?
why is it that martin luther king led the civil rights movement ?	為什麼馬丁路德王領導民權運動 ?
he wasn't the only man who suffered in a precivil rights america , and he certainly wasn't the only great orator of the day .	他不是唯一在美國受過處方權利的男人 , 他肯定不是當天唯一偉大的霸王 。
and why is it that the wright brothers were able to figure out controlled , powered man flight when there were certainly other teams who were better qualified , better funded . . .	為何萊特兄弟能夠想出控制權的男子飛機 , 當時還有其他團隊比較好 , 更好的資金......
and they didn't achieve powered man flight , and the wright brothers beat them to it .	他們沒有達成驅動力的男人飛行 , 萊特兄弟對此打敗了 。
there's something else at play here .	這裡還有別的東西 。
about three and a half years ago i made a discovery .	大約三年半前 , 我做了一個發現 。
and this discovery profoundly changed my view on how i thought the world worked , and it even profoundly changed the way in which i operate in it .	這項發現深深改變了我對世界如何運作的看法 , 甚至徹底改變了我運作的方式 。
as it turns out , there's a pattern .	結果發現 , 有一種模式 。
as it turns out , all the great and inspiring leaders and organizations in the world whether it's apple or martin luther king or the wright brothers they all think , act and communicate the exact same way .	結果發現 , 世界上所有偉大且鼓舞人心的領導者和組織 , 無論是蘋果還是馬丁路德金恩或威特兄弟 , 他們都認為 , 行為和溝通的方式都一樣 。
and it's the complete opposite to everyone else .	這是完全相反的 。
all i did was codify it , and it's probably the world's simplest idea .	我所做的就是將它編碼 , 可能是世界上最簡單的點子 。
i call it the golden circle .	我稱它為黃金圈 。
why ? how ? what ?	為什麼 ? 如何 ? 什麼 ?
this little idea explains why some organizations and some leaders are able to inspire where others aren't .	這個小點子解釋了為什麼有些組織和一些領導者能夠啟發其他人不在哪裡 。
let me define the terms really quickly .	讓我快速定義這個詞 。
every single person , every single organization on the planet knows what they do , 100 percent .	每個人 , 地球上的每個組織都知道他們在做什麼 , 百分之百 。
some know how they do it , whether you call it your differentiated value proposition or your proprietary process or your usp .	有些人知道他們是怎麼辦到的 , 不管你稱它為你的分化價值提議或是你的預先進程或是你的usp 。
but very , very few people or organizations know why they do what they do .	但很少人或組織知道他們為什麼要做他們要做的事 。
and by " why " i don't mean " to make a profit . "	由於 「 為何 」 , 我不是要 「 賺取利潤 」 。
that's a result . it's always a result .	結果就是這樣 。 結果總是如此 。
by " why , " i mean: what's your purpose ?	我的意思是:你的目的是什麼 ?
what's your cause ? what's your belief ?	你的原因是什麼 ? 你的信念是什麼 ?
why does your organization exist ?	你的組織為什麼存在 ?
why do you get out of bed in the morning ?	為何你早上起床 ?
and why should anyone care ?	為什麼有人會在乎呢 ?
well , as a result , the way we think , the way we act , the way we communicate is from the outside in .	因此 , 我們認為我們行為的方式 , 我們溝通的方式來自外界 。
it's obvious . we go from the clearest thing to the fuzziest thing .	這很明顯 。 我們從最清晰的事物到最模糊的事物 。
but the inspired leaders and the inspired organizations regardless of their size , regardless of their industry all think , act and communicate from the inside out .	但激勵領袖和激勵人心的組織 , 不論他們的大小 , 不論他們的產業都在想 , 行動和溝通 。
let me give you an example .	讓我舉個例子 。
i use apple because they're easy to understand and everybody gets it .	我用蘋果 , 因為他們很容易理解 , 每個人都懂 。
if apple were like everyone else , a marketing message from them might sound like this: " we make great computers .	如果蘋果跟其他人一樣 , 一個行銷訊息可能聽起來像這樣: 「 我們製造了很棒的電腦 。
they're beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	他們設計得很漂亮 , 很容易使用和使用者友善 。
want to buy one ? " " meh . "	想買一台嗎 ? " 嘿 ! "
and that's how most of us communicate .	這就是我們大多數人溝通的方式 。
that's how most marketing is done , that's how most sales is done and that's how most of us communicate interpersonally .	這就是多數行銷的方式 , 大部分銷售的做法 , 這就是我們大部分的人之間的溝通方式 。
we say what we do , we say how we're different or how we're better and we expect some sort of a behavior , a purchase , a vote , something like that .	我們會說我們怎麼做 , 我們會說我們是多麼的不一樣 , 我們會預期某種行為、購買、投票 , 等等 。
here's our new law firm: we have the best lawyers with the biggest clients , we always perform for our clients who do business with us .	這是我們的新法律公司:我們有最好的律師和最大的客戶 , 我們總是為我們的客戶做生意 。
here's our new car: it gets great gas mileage , it has leather seats , buy our car .	這是我們的新車 , 大氣里程 , 有皮革的座位 , 購買我們的車 。
here's how apple actually communicates .	蘋果是這樣溝通的 。
" everything we do , we believe in challenging the status quo .	「 我們做的一切 , 我們相信挑戰現狀 。
we believe in thinking differently .	我們用不同的方式相信思考 。
the way we challenge the status quo is by making our products beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	我們挑戰現狀的方式 , 是把我們的產品設計得很漂亮 , 簡單的使用和使用者友善 。
we just happen to make great computers .	我們剛好製造了很棒的電腦 。
want to buy one ? "	想買一台嗎 ? 」
totally different right ? you're ready to buy a computer from me .	完全不同對吧 ? 你準備好要從我身上買一台電腦 。
all i did was reverse the order of the information .	我做的只是逆轉資訊的順序 。
what it proves to us is that people don't buy what you do ; people buy why you do it .	它向我們證明的是 , 人們不買你做什麼 ; 人們買你為什麼要做 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 。
this explains why every single person in this room is perfectly comfortable buying a computer from apple .	這解釋了為什麼在這間房間裡的每個人都很舒服從蘋果買一台電腦 。
but we're also perfectly comfortable buying an mp3 player from apple , or a phone from apple , or a dvr from apple .	但我們也很舒服地買蘋果電腦的mp3玩家 , 或蘋果的手機 , 或蘋果電腦的dvr 。
but , as i said before , apple's just a computer company .	但 , 如我之前所說的 , 蘋果電腦只是一家電腦公司 。
there's nothing that distinguishes them structurally from any of their competitors .	沒有什麼能區別他們和任何競爭者的結構性 。
their competitors are all equally qualified to make all of these products .	他們的競爭者都同樣有資格來製造這些產品 。
in fact , they tried .	事實上 , 他們嘗試了 。
a few years ago , gateway came out with flat screen tvs .	幾年前 , 高速公路上出現了平面的螢幕電視 。
they're eminently qualified to make flat screen tvs .	他們很有資格來製作平面電視 。
they've been making flat screen monitors for years .	多年來 , 他們一直在製作平面螢幕螢幕 。
dell came out with mp3 players and pdas , and they make great quality products , and they can make perfectly welldesigned products and nobody bought one .	迪爾帶著mp3玩家和帕德斯出櫃 , 他們製作了很棒的品質產品 , 他們可以做出非常好的設計產品 , 沒有人買 。
in fact , talking about it now , we can't even imagine buying an mp3 player from dell .	事實上 , 談到現在 , 我們甚至無法想像 , 買了來自德雷爾的mp3播放器 。
why would you buy an mp3 player from a computer company ?	你為什麼要從一家電腦公司買個mp3玩家呢 ?
but we do it every day .	但我們每天都這樣做 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 。
the goal is not to do business with everybody who needs what you have .	目標不是要和所有需要你的東西做生意 。
the goal is to do business with people who believe what you believe .	目標是要和那些相信你所相信的人做生意 。
here's the best part: none of what i'm telling you is my opinion .	最好的部分是:我所說的 , 沒有一個是我的意見 。
it's all grounded in the tenets of biology .	一切都基於生物學的基礎 。
not psychology , biology .	不是心理學、生物學 。
if you look at a crosssection of the human brain , looking from the top down , what you see is the human brain is actually broken into three major components that correlate perfectly with the golden circle .	如果你仔細觀察人腦的十字路口 , 從頭向下看 , 你看到的是人類的大腦其實分裂成三個主要元件 , 完全與黃金圈結合 。
our newest brain , our homo sapien brain , our neocortex , corresponds with the " what " level .	我們最新的大腦 , 我們的智人腦 , 我們的新皮質 , 會對應 「 什麼 」 的程度 。
the neocortex is responsible for all of our rational and analytical thought and language .	新皮層負責所有理性、分析思維和語言 。
the middle two sections make up our limbic brains , and our limbic brains are responsible for all of our feelings , like trust and loyalty .	中間的兩個部分構成了我們的腦 , 我們的肢體大腦負責我們所有的感覺 , 像是信任和忠誠 。
it's also responsible for all human behavior , all decisionmaking , and it has no capacity for language .	它也要為所有人類行為負責 , 所有決策 , 且它沒有語言的能力 。
in other words , when we communicate from the outside in , yes , people can understand vast amounts of complicated information like features and benefits and facts and figures .	換句話說 , 當我們從外面溝通時 , 是的 , 人們可以了解大量複雜的資訊 , 比如特徵、利益、事實和數字 。
it just doesn't drive behavior .	它不會驅動行為 。
when we can communicate from the inside out , we're talking directly to the part of the brain that controls behavior , and then we allow people to rationalize it with the tangible things we say and do .	當我們可以從內部溝通時 , 我們直接和控制行為的大腦溝通 , 然後我們允許人們用我們所說和做的事來合理化 。
this is where gut decisions come from .	這就是腸子決定的來源 。
you know , sometimes you can give somebody all the facts and figures , and they say , " i know what all the facts and details say , but it just doesn't feel right . "	有時 , 你可以給某人所有事實和數字 , 他們說: 「 我知道所有事實和細節都說了什麼 , 但感覺不對 。 」
why would we use that verb , it doesn't " feel " right ?	為什麼我們會用那個動詞 , 感覺不對 ?
because the part of the brain that controls decisionmaking doesn't control language .	因為控制決策的部分無法控制語言 。
and the best we can muster up is , " i don't know . it just doesn't feel right . "	最好的是我們能忍受的是: 「 我不知道 , 感覺不對 。 」
or sometimes you say you're leading with your heart , or you're leading with your soul .	或有時你會說你在帶著你的心 , 或你帶著你的靈魂去領導 。
well , i hate to break it to you , those aren't other body parts controlling your behavior .	嗯 , 我討厭打破它 , 不是其他身體部位控制你的行為 。
it's all happening here in your limbic brain , the part of the brain that controls decisionmaking and not language .	這一切都在你的腦袋裡發生 , 大腦控制決策的部位 , 而非語言 。
but if you don't know why you do what you do , and people respond to why you do what you do , then how will you ever get people to vote for you , or buy something from you , or , more importantly , be loyal and want to be a part of what it is that you do .	但如果你不知道你為什麼要做你要做的事 , 大家會回應為什麼要做你要做的事 , 那麼你要如何讓人們為你投票 , 或更重要的是忠誠 , 想要成為你所做的事的一部分 。
again , the goal is not just to sell to people who need what you have ; the goal is to sell to people who believe what you believe .	同樣的 , 目標不只是賣給需要你所擁有的東西的人 ; 目標是要賣給那些相信你所相信的人 。
the goal is not just to hire people who need a job ; it's to hire people who believe what you believe .	目標不只是要僱用需要工作的人 , 而是僱用那些相信你所相信的人們 。
i always say that , you know , if you hire people just because they can do a job , they'll work for your money , but if you hire people who believe what you believe , they'll work for you with blood and sweat and tears .	我總是說 , 如果你雇用別人 , 只因為他們能做一份工作 , 他們會為你的錢工作 , 但如果你雇用那些相信你所相信的人 , 他們會為你工作 , 用血汗和淚水 。
and nowhere else is there a better example of this than with the wright brothers .	沒有比萊特兄弟更好的例子 。
most people don't know about samuel pierpont langley .	大多數人不知道samuelpierpontlangley 。
and back in the early 20th century , the pursuit of powered man flight was like the dot com of the day .	在二十世紀初 , 追求驅動人類飛行的追求就像是日常的 「 點 」 。
everybody was trying it .	每個人都在嘗試 。
and samuel pierpont langley had , what we assume , to be the recipe for success .	而samuelpierpontlangley認為我們是成功的食譜 。
i mean , even now , you ask people , " why did your product or why did your company fail ? "	我的意思是 , 甚至現在 , 你問人們: 「 為什麼你的產品或為什麼你的公司會失敗 ? 」
and people always give you the same permutation of the same three things: undercapitalized , the wrong people , bad market conditions .	人們總是會給你相同的三件事:被破壞、錯誤的人、不好的市場條件 。
it's always the same three things , so let's explore that .	一直都是一樣的三件事 , 讓我們來探索一下 。
samuel pierpont langley was given 50 , 000 dollars by the war department to figure out this flying machine .	samuelpierpontlangley給了五萬美金 , 由戰爭部門提供了這台飛行機 。
money was no problem .	金錢不是問題 。
he held a seat at harvard and worked at the smithsonian and was extremely wellconnected ; he knew all the big minds of the day .	他在哈佛舉辦了一座座椅 , 在史密森尼工作 , 非常有連結 , 他知道當天的所有大人 。
he hired the best minds money could find and the market conditions were fantastic .	他雇用了最好的思想金錢 , 找到市場條件很棒 。
the new york times followed him around everywhere , and everyone was rooting for langley .	紐約時報隨後到處追蹤他 , 每個人都在為langley打擊 。
then how come we've never heard of samuel pierpont langley ?	為什麼我們從來沒有聽過samuelpierpontlangley ?
a few hundred miles away in dayton ohio , orville and wilbur wright , they had none of what we consider to be the recipe for success .	離俄亥俄州幾百英里外 , 奧維爾和威爾堡萊特 , 他們沒有我們認為成功的秘訣 。
they had no money ; they paid for their dream with the proceeds from their bicycle shop ; not a single person on the wright brothers' team had a college education , not even orville or wilbur ; and the new york times followed them around nowhere .	他們沒有錢 , 他們付了他們的夢想 , 拿著自行車店的執行長 ; 萊特兄弟的團隊裡沒有一個人有大學教育 , 甚至不是奧維爾或威爾堡 ; 紐約時報隨他們到處走 。
the difference was , orville and wilbur were driven by a cause , by a purpose , by a belief .	不同之處在於 , 俄維爾和威爾堡被一個理由所驅使 , 由一個有目的的 , 由一個想法所驅使 。
they believed that if they could figure out this flying machine , it'll change the course of the world .	他們相信如果他們能弄清楚這台飛行機器 , 它會改變世界的軌道 。
samuel pierpont langley was different .	samuelpierpontlangley不同 。
he wanted to be rich , and he wanted to be famous .	他想要變得富有 , 他想要有名 。
he was in pursuit of the result .	他在追求結果 。
he was in pursuit of the riches .	他在追求富人 。
and lo and behold , look what happened .	看 , 看看發生了什麼事 。
the people who believed in the wright brothers' dream worked with them with blood and sweat and tears .	相信萊特兄弟的夢想與他們一起工作 , 帶著血液、汗水和淚水 。
the others just worked for the paycheck .	其他人只是為了支付而工作 。
and they tell stories of how every time the wright brothers went out , they would have to take five sets of parts , because that's how many times they would crash before they came in for supper .	他們會說故事 , 關於每次萊特兄弟出門時 , 他們就得拿五組零件 , 因為他們在供應商之前會衝擊多少次 。
and , eventually , on december 17th , 1903 , the wright brothers took flight , and no one was there to even experience it .	最後 , 在1903年12月17日 , 萊特兄弟搭飛機 , 沒有人會去體驗它 。
we found out about it a few days later .	幾天後 , 我們發現了這件事 。
and further proof that langley was motivated by the wrong thing: the day the wright brothers took flight , he quit .	更進一步的證明 , 萊特兄弟踏上飛機的那天 , 他辭掉了 。
he could have said , " that's an amazing discovery , guys , and i will improve upon your technology , " but he didn't .	他可以說: 「 那是個很棒的發現 , 各位 , 我會改善你的技術 。 」 但他沒有 。
he wasn't first , he didn't get rich , he didn't get famous so he quit .	他沒有第一 , 他沒有富有 , 他沒有出名 , 所以他辭掉了 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 。
and if you talk about what you believe , you will attract those who believe what you believe .	如果你談到你所相信的 , 你就會吸引那些相信你所相信的人 。
but why is it important to attract those who believe what you believe ?	但為什麼要吸引那些相信你所相信的你是很重要的呢 ?
something called the law of diffusion of innovation , and if you don't know the law , you definitely know the terminology .	一種叫做 「 創新法則 」 , 如果你不知道法律 , 你肯定知道 「 創新法則 」 。
the first two and a half percent of our population are our innovators .	前2.5%的人口是我們的創新者 。
the next 13 and a half percent of our population are our early adopters .	接下來的13.5%是我們早期的採用者 。
the next 34 percent are your early majority , your late majority and your laggards .	接下來的34%是你最早期 , 大部分是遲到的 , 和你的遲緩 。
the only reason these people buy touch tone phones is because you can't buy rotary phones anymore .	這些人只買觸覺電話的唯一理由 , 是因為你再也買不到輪椅手機了 。
we all sit at various places at various times on this scale , but what the law of diffusion of innovation tells us is that if you want massmarket success or massmarket acceptance of an idea , you cannot have it until you achieve this tipping point between 15 and 18 percent market penetration , and then the system tips .	我們都坐在不同的階段 , 但創新的傳播法則告訴我們 , 如果你想要大規模市場的成功 , 或大眾市場接受這個點子 , 直到你達成了15%到18%的市場退休金之間的轉捩點 , 接著 , 系統的秘密 。
and i love asking businesses , " what's your conversion on new business ? "	我喜歡問企業: 「 你對新生意的轉變是什麼 ? 」
and they love to tell you , " oh , it's about 10 percent , " proudly .	他們很愛告訴你: 「 喔 , 大約是10% 。 」 驕傲地說 。
well , you can trip over 10 percent of the customers .	嗯 , 你可以試超過10%的客戶 。
we all have about 10 percent who just " get it . "	我們都有大約10%的 「 得到它 」 。
that's how we describe them , right ?	我們就是這樣描述他們 , 對吧 ?
that's like that gut feeling , " oh , they just get it . "	那就像是那種直覺 , 「 喔 , 他們剛好懂了 。 」
the problem is: how do you find the ones that get it before you're doing business with them versus the ones who don't get it ?	問題是:你要如何在你和他們做生意之前找到那些能得到的 ?
so it's this here , this little gap that you have to close , as jeffrey moore calls it , " crossing the chasm " because , you see , the early majority will not try something until someone else has tried it first .	所以 , 在這裡 , 這個小小的鴻溝 , 如傑佛瑞•摩爾稱它為 「 跨越魅力 」 , 因為 , 你看 , 早期的大多數人 , 直到別人先試過它 。
and these guys , the innovators and the early adopters , they're comfortable making those gut decisions .	這些人 , 創新者和早期採用者 , 他們很自在地做出那些直覺決策 。
they're more comfortable making those intuitive decisions that are driven by what they believe about the world and not just what product is available .	他們比較自在地做出那些直覺的決策 , 由他們對世界的信念所驅使 , 而不只是產品能取得的 。
these are the people who stood in line for six hours to buy an iphone when they first came out , when you could have just walked into the store the next week and bought one off the shelf .	這些人 , 第一次出櫃時 , 站了六個小時 , 買一支iphone , 當你走進商店 , 下週買了一台貨架 。
these are the people who spent 40 , 000 dollars on flat screen tvs when they first came out , even though the technology was substandard .	這些人 , 首次在平面電視上花了四萬美金 , 即便科技是 「 隨便 」 。
and , by the way , they didn't do it because the technology was so great ; they did it for themselves .	順帶一提 , 他們沒有這麼做 , 因為科技太棒了 , 他們為自己做了 。
it's because they wanted to be first .	那是因為他們想成為第一的 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it and what you do simply proves what you believe .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 , 以及你所做的 , 證明你所相信的 。
in fact , people will do the things that prove what they believe .	事實上 , 人們會做那些證明他們所相信的事 。
the reason that person bought the iphone in the first six hours , stood in line for six hours , was because of what they believed about the world , and how they wanted everybody to see them: they were first .	一個人在六小時內買了iphone , 站在六個小時 , 是因為他們對世界的信念 , 以及他們想讓每個人看見他們:他們是第一個 。
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 。
so let me give you a famous example , a famous failure and a famous success of the law of diffusion of innovation .	讓我舉一個有名的例子 , 一個有名的失敗以及一個有名的成功 , 關於創新的傳播法則 。
first , the famous failure .	首先 , 著名的失敗 。
it's a commercial example .	這是一個商業的例子 。
as we said before , a second ago , the recipe for success is money and the right people and the right market conditions , right ? you should have success then .	如我們先前所說 , 成功的食譜是金錢、對的人、對的市場條件 , 對吧 ? 你當時應該要成功 。
from the time tivo came out about eight or nine years ago to this current day , they are the single highestquality product on the market , hands down , there is no dispute .	從八、九年前到現在 , 他們是市場上最高品質的產品 , 下降 , 沒有爭議 。
they were extremely wellfunded .	他們非常受歡迎 。
market conditions were fantastic .	市場條件很棒 。
i mean , we use tivo as verb .	我的意思是 , 我們把tivo當作動詞 。
i tivo stuff on my piece of junk time warner dvr all the time .	我經常在垃圾筒裡提取一些東西 , 用我的垃圾時間華納的dvr 。
but tivo's a commercial failure .	但tivo是一種商業失敗 。
they've never made money .	他們從來沒有賺錢 。
and when they went ipo , their stock was at about 30 or 40 dollars and then plummeted , and it's never traded above 10 .	當他們去ipo時 , 他們的股票大約是30或40塊美金 , 然後被量化了 , 從來沒有交易超過10元 。
in fact , i don't think it's even traded above six , except for a couple of little spikes .	事實上 , 我不認為它在六歲以上交易 , 只不過有幾次小爆炸 。
because you see , when tivo launched their product they told us all what they had .	因為你看 , 當tivo發表他們的產品時 , 他們告訴我們他們所擁有的 。
they said , " we have a product that pauses live tv , skips commercials , rewinds live tv and memorizes your viewing habits without you even asking . "	他們說: 「 我們有一種產品 , 暫停現場電視、滑雪廣告、再生現場電視 , 還記住你看的習慣 , 甚至不需要你問 。 」
and the cynical majority said , " we don't believe you .	絕大多數的憤世嫉俗說: 「 我們不相信你 。
we don't need it . we don't like it .	我們不需要它 。 我們不喜歡它 。
you're scaring us . "	你嚇了我們 。 」
what if they had said , " if you're the kind of person who likes to have total control over every aspect of your life , boy , do we have a product for you .	如果他們說: 「 若你是那種喜歡完全控制你的人生的那種人 , 男孩 , 我們是否有產品給你 。
it pauses live tv , skips commercials , memorizes your viewing habits , etc . , etc . "	它會暫停現場電視、滑雪廣告 , 記住你看的習慣 , 諸如此類 。 」
people don't buy what you do ; they buy why you do it , and what you do simply serves as the proof of what you believe .	人們不買你做什麼 ; 他們買你為什麼要做 , 而你所做的就是證明你所相信的 。
now let me give you a successful example of the law of diffusion of innovation .	現在 , 讓我給各位一個成功的例子 , 關於創新的傳播法則 。
in the summer of 1963 , 250 , 000 people showed up on the mall in washington to hear dr . king speak .	1963年夏天 , 有25萬人出現在華盛頓的商場上 , 聽見金恩博士演講 。
they sent out no invitations , and there was no website to check the date .	他們沒有邀請 , 也沒有網站來檢查約會 。
how do you do that ?	你怎麼做呢 ?
well , dr . king wasn't the only man in america who was a great orator .	嗯 , 金恩博士不是美國唯一一個偉大的演員 。
he wasn't the only man in america who suffered in a precivil rights america .	他不是唯一在美國受過處方權利的男人 。
in fact , some of his ideas were bad .	事實上 , 他的一些想法很糟 。
but he had a gift .	但他有一個禮物 。
he didn't go around telling people what needed to change in america .	他沒有四處四處告訴人們在美國所需的改變 。
he went around and told people what he believed .	他四處走來告訴人們他所相信的 。
" i believe , i believe , i believe , " he told people .	「 我相信 , 我相信 , 我相信 , 」 他告訴別人 。
and people who believed what he believed took his cause , and they made it their own , and they told people .	而相信他所相信的人們 , 把他的理由拿出來 , 他們自己做出來 , 他們告訴人們 。
and some of those people created structures to get the word out to even more people .	其中一些人創造了結構 , 讓更多人知道這個詞 。
and lo and behold , 250 , 000 people showed up on the right day at the right time to hear him speak .	沒錯 , 有25萬人在正確的日子出現 , 聽到他說話 。
how many of them showed up for him ?	其中有多少人為他出席 ?
they showed up for themselves .	他們為自己出現 。
it's what they believed about america that got them to travel in a bus for eight hours to stand in the sun in washington in the middle of august .	他們相信美國能讓他們在車上旅行八小時 , 站在華盛頓的陽光下 。
it's what they believed , and it wasn't about black versus white: 25 percent of the audience was white .	這是他們所相信的 , 重點不是黑人和白人:25%的觀眾是白人 。
dr . king believed that there are two types of laws in this world: those that are made by a higher authority and those that are made by man .	金恩博士相信世上有兩種法則:用更高的權威和那些由人類所組成的法律 。
and not until all the laws that are made by man are consistent with the laws that are made by the higher authority will we live in a just world .	直到人類所制定的所有法則 , 都與更高權威的法律一致 , 我們將活在一個正義的世界 。
it just so happened that the civil rights movement was the perfect thing to help him bring his cause to life .	剛好 , 民權運動是幫助他把他的成因帶給他 。
we followed , not for him , but for ourselves .	我們追隨了 , 不是為了他 , 而是為了我們自己 。
and , by the way , he gave the " i have a dream " speech , not the " i have a plan " speech .	順便一提 , 他給了 「 我有一個夢想 」 演講 , 不是 「 我有計畫 」 演講 。
listen to politicians now , with their comprehensive 12point plans .	現在聽聽政治人物 , 用他們全面的12點計畫 。
they're not inspiring anybody .	他們沒有鼓舞任何人 。
because there are leaders and there are those who lead .	因為有領導者和領導者 。
leaders hold a position of power or authority , but those who lead inspire us .	領導者持有權力或權威的立場 , 但領導者鼓舞了我們 。
whether they're individuals or organizations , we follow those who lead , not because we have to , but because we want to .	不論是個人或組織 , 我們遵守領導者 , 不是因為我們必須這麼做 , 而是因為我們想要 。
we follow those who lead , not for them , but for ourselves .	我們追蹤那些領導的人 , 不是為了他們 , 而是為了我們自己 。
and it's those who start with " why " that have the ability to inspire those around them or find others who inspire them .	是那些從 「 為什麼 」 開始的人 , 能夠鼓舞他們身邊的人 , 或找到鼓舞他們的人 。
how do you remember where you parked your car ? how do you know if you're moving in the right direction ? neuroscientist neil burgess studies the neural mechanisms that map the space around us , and how they link to memory and imagination .	你還記得你在哪裡停車 ? 你要怎麼知道你要移動正確的方向 ? 神經科學家神經學家研究了我們周遭的神經機制 , 以及他們如何連結記憶和想像力 。
brain , cognitive science , exploration , neuroscience , science	大腦、認知科學、探索、神經科學、科學、科學、科學 。
neil burgess: how your brain tells you where you are	尼爾堡:你的大腦如何告訴你你在哪裡 。
when we park in a big parking lot , how do we remember where we parked our car ?	當我們在一個大停車場停車場時 , 我們要怎麼記得我們停車的地方 ?
here's the problem facing homer .	問題來了 , 面對家長的問題 。
and we're going to try to understand what's happening in his brain .	我們要試著去了解他的大腦發生了什麼事 。
so we'll start with the hippocampus , shown in yellow , which is the organ of memory .	我們先從海馬體開始 , 向黃色展示 , 這是記憶的器官 。
if you have damage there , like in alzheimer's , you can't remember things including where you parked your car .	如果你有損傷 , 像阿茲海默症 , 你無法記住東西 , 包括你停車的地方 。
it's named after latin for " seahorse , " which it resembles .	它是以 「 海馬 」 為名的拉丁文 , 它是相似的 。
and like the rest of the brain , it's made of neurons .	就像大腦的其他部分 , 它是由神經元組成的 。
so the human brain has about a hundred billion neurons in it .	人類的大腦大約有一千億個神經元 。
and the neurons communicate with each other by sending little pulses or spikes of electricity via connections to each other .	神經元彼此溝通 , 藉由發送細小的脈衝或電刺激 , 來彼此連結 。
the hippocampus is formed of two sheets of cells , which are very densely interconnected .	海馬體是由兩片細胞組成 , 非常密集的相互連結 。
and scientists have begun to understand how spatial memory works by recording from individual neurons in rats or mice while they forage or explore an environment looking for food .	科學家開始了解空間記憶如何運作 , 藉由記錄老鼠或老鼠的個別神經元 , 來探索尋找食物的環境 。
so we're going to imagine we're recording from a single neuron in the hippocampus of this rat here .	所以 , 我們要想像我們從這隻老鼠的海馬體中記錄一個單一個神經元 。
and when it fires a little spike of electricity , there's going to be a red dot and a click .	當它發出電量時 , 就會有一個紅點和點擊 。
so what we see is that this neuron knows whenever the rat has gone into one particular place in its environment .	我們看到的是 , 這種神經元知道 , 每當老鼠進入一個特定的環境中時 , 老鼠就知道了 。
and it signals to the rest of the brain by sending a little electrical spike .	大腦其他部位會透過發送小小的電擊訊號傳送訊息給大腦 。
so we could show the firing rate of that neuron as a function of the animal's location .	所以 , 我們可以把神經元的發射速度顯示為動物的位置 。
and if we record from lots of different neurons , we'll see that different neurons fire when the animal goes in different parts of its environment , like in this square box shown here .	如果我們從許多不同的神經元中記錄下來 , 我們會發現當動物在環境中的不同區域移動時 , 像這個正方形的盒子裡 。
so together they form a map for the rest of the brain , telling the brain continually , " where am i now within my environment ? "	所以 , 他們一起為大腦其餘的部分建立了一張地圖 , 不斷地告訴大腦: 「 我現在在我的環境中哪裡 ? 」
place cells are also being recorded in humans .	位置細胞也被記錄在人體中 。
so epilepsy patients sometimes need the electrical activity in their brain monitoring .	所以癲癇患者有時會需要腦部監控的電活動 。
and some of these patients played a video game where they drive around a small town .	有些病人玩了一個電玩遊戲 , 讓他們在一個小鎮開車 。
and place cells in their hippocampi would fire , become active , start sending electrical impulses whenever they drove through a particular location in that town .	把它們的嬉皮植入細胞 , 會被激發 , 開始發送電子衝動 , 不論如何穿越某個特定的位置 。
so how does a place cell know where the rat or person is within its environment ?	所以 , 一個地方細胞怎麼知道老鼠或人在環境中的位置 ?
well these two cells here show us that the boundaries of the environment are particularly important .	這兩個細胞告訴我們 , 環境的邊界是非常重要的 。
so the one on the top likes to fire sort of midway between the walls of the box that their rat's in .	所以 , 上面的那隻 , 像是在盒子裡的老鼠牆壁上開火 ,
and when you expand the box , the firing location expands .	當你擴大盒子時 , 發射所在的位置就會擴大 。
the one below likes to fire whenever there's a wall close by to the south .	下面的那一面 , 只要有一面牆靠近南方 。
and if you put another wall inside the box , then the cell fires in both place wherever there's a wall to the south as the animal explores around in its box .	如果你把另一面牆放在箱子裡 , 細胞就會在兩個地方發射 , 無論在裡面有一面牆 , 作為動物在盒子裡四處探索的 。
so this predicts that sensing the distances and directions of boundaries around you extended buildings and so on is particularly important for the hippocampus .	這種預測 , 會感應到周圍的邊界線和方向 , 延伸到大樓之外 , 尤其對海馬體來說是很重要的 。
and indeed , on the inputs to the hippocampus , cells are found which project into the hippocampus , which do respond exactly to detecting boundaries or edges at particular distances and directions from the rat or mouse as it's exploring around .	的確 , 在海馬體的輸入上 , 細胞會在海馬體中找到哪個項目 , 會反應出偵測邊界或邊緣 , 尤其是在老鼠或老鼠四處探索時的方向 。
so the cell on the left , you can see , it fires whenever the animal gets near to a wall or a boundary to the east , whether it's the edge or the wall of a square box or the circular wall of the circular box or even the drop at the edge of a table , which the animals are running around .	左邊的細胞 , 你可以看到 , 每當動物靠近一面牆或一道向東邊的邊界 , 不論是方形或圓形的牆 , 或甚至是桌子邊緣的圓形牆 。
and the cell on the right there fires whenever there's a boundary to the south , whether it's the drop at the edge of the table or a wall or even the gap between two tables that are pulled apart .	右邊的細胞 , 每當南方有邊界時 , 不論是桌面或牆的邊緣 , 或甚至兩個桌子之間的落差 。
so that's one way in which we think place cells determine where the animal is as it's exploring around .	所以這就是我們認為讓細胞決定動物在周圍探索時的位置 。
we can also test where we think objects are , like this goal flag , in simple environments or indeed , where your car would be .	我們也能測試我們認為物體的位置 , 例如這個目標旗 , 在簡單的環境中 , 或你的車會在哪裡 。
so we can have people explore an environment and see the location they have to remember .	所以 , 我們可以讓人們去探索一個環境 , 看看他們要記得的位置 。
and then , if we put them back in the environment , generally they're quite good at putting a marker down where they thought that flag or their car was .	然後 , 如果我們把它們放回環境中 , 通常它們很擅長把標記放到他們認為旗幟或車子的位置上 。
but on some trials , we could change the shape and size of the environment like we did with the place cell .	但在某些試驗中 , 我們可以改變環境的形狀和大小 , 就像我們用定位細胞一樣 。
in that case , we can see how where they think the flag had been changes as a function of how you change the shape and size of the environment .	在這個例子中 , 我們可以看到他們認為旗幟的位置是如何改變你如何改變環境的形狀和尺寸 。
and what you see , for example , if the flag was where that cross was in a small square environment , and then if you ask people where it was , but you've made the environment bigger , where they think the flag had been stretches out in exactly the same way that the place cell firing stretched out .	舉例來說 , 如果你的旗幟在一個小方形的環境中 , 你可以看到 , 如果問人們在哪裡 , 但你已經讓環境變大 , 他們認為旗幟已經完全相同 , 細胞發射出來的位置 。
it's as if you remember where the flag was by storing the pattern of firing across all of your place cells at that location , and then you can get back to that location by moving around so that you best match the current pattern of firing of your place cells with that stored pattern .	這就好像你還記得旗幟的位置 , 藉著儲存所有位置細胞的模式 , 儲存在你所在位置的位置 , 然後你就可以回到那個位置 , 這樣你就能最好配合你位置細胞的目前模式 , 以儲存的模式 。
that guides you back to the location that you want to remember .	那會引導你回到你想要記得的地點 。
but we also know where we are through movement .	但我們也知道我們在運動的方向 。
so if we take some outbound path perhaps we park and we wander off we know because our own movements , which we can integrate over this path roughly what the heading direction is to go back .	所以如果我們採取一些外界的路徑 , 或許我們停下來 , 我們就會知道 , 因為我們自己的動作 , 我們可以將這條路徑整合起來 , 大概可以回頭去 。
and place cells also get this kind of path integration input from a kind of cell called a grid cell .	位置細胞也得到這種通路的整合輸入 , 來自一種叫做網狀細胞的細胞 。
